                <div class="story-photo">

                </div>
                <div class="story-content">
                 <h2 class="story-title">
                  <a href="/article/us-health-coronavirus-india-cases/massive-religious-gathering-worries-india-as-covid-19-cases-surge-idUSKBN2BD07M" target="_self">
                   Massive religious gathering worries India as COVID-19 cases surge
                  </a>
                 </h2>
                 <div class="byline">
                 </div>
                 <p>
                  The health ministry said up to 40 people were testing positive for daily around the site of the weeks-long Mahakumbh gathering that began this month and peaks in April. The festival is held once every 12 years and organizers have said more than 150 million visitors are expected.
                 </p>
                 <ul>
                  <li>
                   <a href="/article/us-health-coronavirus-indonesia/astrazeneca-counters-indonesian-muslim-concerns-over-covid-19-vaccine-idUSKBN2BD02X" target="_self">

                   </a>
                  </li>
                  <li>
                   <a href="/article/us-health-coronavirus-denmark/denmark-reports-two-cases-of-serious-illness-including-one-death-after-astrazeneca-shot-idUSKBN2BC0A4" target="_self">

                   </a>
                  </li>

//Sponsor data array
const sponsors = new Array;

//Render container and push ad data to sponsors array
function renderSponsorContainer(id, type, el) {
	const sponsor_container = document.createElement('div');
	sponsor_container.id = id;
	sponsor_container.className = 'gpt-sponsored-mod';

	//Append container
	el.appendChild(sponsor_container);

	//Push to sponsors
	sponsors.push({
		el_id: id,
		ad_type: type
	});
}

// Check for keyowrds
for (i=0; featured_headings.length > i; i++) {
	const text = featured_headings[i].innerText.toLowerCase().trim();
	switch(text) {

		// LIFE LESSONS
		case 'life lessons':
			renderSponsorContainer('adSponsorLifeLessons', 'llmodule', featured_headings[i]); 
			break;

		// BREAKINGVIEWS
		case 'breakingviews':
			renderSponsorContainer('adSponsorBreakingviews', 'breakingviewsmodulelogo', featured_headings[i]);
			break;

		// TWITTER CHAT
		case 'twitter chat':
		case 'chats: reuters charity':
			renderSponsorContainer('adSponsorChat', 'tc_module', featured_headings[i]);
			break;

		// EXCHANGE-TRADED FUNDS
		case 'exchange-traded funds':
                case 'etfs':
			renderSponsorContainer('adSponsorETFs', 'etf_module', featured_headings[i]);
			break;

		// SECTORS UP CLOSE
		case 'sectors up close':
                case 'sectors upclose':
			renderSponsorContainer('adSponsorSectors', 'sector_module', featured_headings[i]);
			break;

		// INVESTING
		case 'investing':
			renderSponsorContainer('adSponsorInvesting', 'investingmodule', featured_headings[i]);
			break;

		// WORLD AT WORK
		case 'world at work':
                case 'the world at work':
			renderSponsorContainer('adSponsorWorldAtWork', 'wowmodule', featured_headings[i]);
			break;

		// AIRBUS
                case 'aerospace':
                case 'aerospace & defense':
		case 'farnborough airshow':
                case 'paris airshow':
                case 'paris air show':
			renderSponsorContainer('adSponsorAirbus', 'airbusmodule', featured_headings[i]);
			break;

		// DAVOS
                case 'davos':
		case 'davos coverage':
                case 'davos 2020':
			renderSponsorContainer('adSponsorDavos', 'davmodule', featured_headings[i]);
			break;

		// FUTURE OF MONEY
		case 'future of money':
		case 'the future of money':
			renderSponsorContainer('adSponsorFutureOfMoney', 'fom_hp_module', featured_headings[i]);
			break;
            
		// THE Z FACTOR
		case 'the z factor':
			renderSponsorContainer('adSponsorTheZFactor', 'zfac_hp_module', featured_headings[i]);
		  	break;

		// ESG
		case 'sustainable business':
		  	renderSponsorContainer('adSponsorESG', 'esgmodule', featured_headings[i]);
		  	break;

		// FORWARD
		case 'forward':
		  	renderSponsorContainer('adSponsorForward', 'forwardmodule', featured_headings[i]);
		  	break;

		// MILKEN CONFERENCE
		case 'milken conference':
		  	renderSponsorContainer('adSponsorForward', 'milkenlogo', featured_headings[i]);
		  	break;

		// SOHN INVESTMENT CONFERENCE
		case 'sohn investment conference':
		  	renderSponsorContainer('adSponsorForward', 'sohnmod', featured_headings[i]);
		  	break;

		// ECONOMY
		case 'economy':
		  	renderSponsorContainer('adSponsorForward', 'economylogo', featured_headings[i]);
		  	break;    

		// CANCER AND COVID-19
		case 'cancer and covid-19':
		  	renderSponsorContainer('adSponsorForward', 'cancercaresmod', featured_headings[i]);
		  	break;

		// THE GREAT REBOOT
		case 'the great reboot':
		  	renderSponsorContainer('adSponsorForward', 'greatreboot', featured_headings[i]);
		  	break;    
            
	}
}

// Display ads
sponsors.forEach((s) => {
	displayAd(s.el_id, TR3.extractDartZone(), [[186,24]], "type="+s.ad_type+";"+adParams2 );
})
